No rounding is applied.\n    58→\n    59→**Triage**: Must-resolve `[Blocking Phase 5]`\n    60→\n    61→**Rationale**: The roadmap Phase 5 explicitly states: \"Downstream readiness gate: `overall >= 7.0` (boundary: 7.0 true, 6.9 false).\" The SC-009 validation criterion confirms: \"Downstream: 7.0 true, 6.9 false.\" The overall score is computed as the arithmetic mean of 4 quality dimensions (clarity, completeness, testability, consistency), and the comparison uses `>=` with no rounding. This means:\n    62→- `overall = 7.0` -> gate passes\n    63→- `overall = 6.99999` -> gate fails\n    64→- `overall = 7.0001` -> gate passes\n    65→- Arithmetic precision is maintained to at least 2 decimal places (+/-0.01 per SC-008).\n    66→\n    67→**Impact on gate implementation**: The gate function must use `>=` comparison with no rounding. The SC-008 criterion (\"Overall = mean(4 dimensions) +/-0.01\") defines the acceptable precision tolerance for the arithmetic computation, not a rounding policy for gate evaluation.\n    68→\n    69→**Source**: Roadmap Phase 5, Work Item 3; SC-008 and SC-009 validation criteria.\n    70→\n    71→---\n    72→\n    73→## Resolution 4: Authoritative Module Layout\n    74→\n    75→**Question**: Section 4.1 (13 files) vs. Section 4.6 (roadmap 18 modules) -- which is authoritative?\n    76→\n    77→**Decision**: 18-module structure per DEV-001 accepted deviation is authoritative. Each decision includes rationale derived from roadmap text or DEV-001, and is triaged as must-resolve, safe-default, or defer-to-follow-up with blocking-phase annotations.\n\n---\n\n## Resolution 1: Timeout Semantics for Convergence Iterations\n\n**Question**: Per-iteration independent timeout vs. total timeout divided by `max_convergence`?\n\n**Decision**: Per-iteration independent timeout (default 300s).\n\n**Triage**: Must-resolve `[Blocking Phase 5]`\n\n**Rationale**: The roadmap Phase 5 explicitly states: \"Per-iteration independent timeout (default 300s, per Phase 0 decision).\" Each convergence iteration in `panel-review` (Step 7) receives its own independent 300-second timeout. This means that if `max_convergence=3`, the theoretical maximum wall-clock time for the convergence loop is 3 x 300s = 900s, not 300s / 3 = 100s per iteration.\n\n**Impact on `PortifyConfig`**: Requires a single `iteration_timeout` field (default 300s). No separate `total_budget` field is needed for timeout semantics. The `max_convergence` field controls iteration count, not timeout division.\n\n**Source**: Roadmap Phase 5, Work Item 3 (panel-review); SC-016 validation criterion.\n\n---\n\n## Resolution 2: Resume Behavior for Partially Written `synthesize-spec`\n\n**Question**: Re-run `synthesize-spec` vs. skip when output is partial?\n\n**Decision**: Prefer re-running `synthesize-spec` over trusting partially gated output.\n\n**Triage**: Must-resolve `[Blocking Phase 4]`\n\n**Rationale**: The roadmap Phase 4, Work Item 3 (synthesize-spec) explicitly states: \"Resume policy: prefer re-running `synthesize-spec` over trusting partially gated output (per Phase 0 decision).\" A partially written spec that failed its STRICT gate (SC-005: zero remaining `{{SC_PLACEHOLDER:*}}` sentinels) cannot be trusted. no truncation of partial logs |\n\n---\n\n## Frontmatter Rules\n\n### Parsing Behavior\n\n1. YAML frontmatter is delimited by `---` on its own line at the start and end of the frontmatter block.\n2. Frontmatter must appear at the very beginning of the file (line 1).\n3. Missing frontmatter in a file that requires it is a gate failure.\n4. Unknown frontmatter fields are ignored (forward-compatible).\n5. Required fields that are missing cause a gate failure with a diagnostic message naming the missing field(s).\n\n### Validation Behavior\n\n1. Type validation: fields must match their declared types (string, int, float, bool).\n2. Range validation: count fields must be >= 0; score fields must be 0.0-10.0.\n3. Semantic validation: per-gate SC criteria (e.g., SC-003 requires 5 specific frontmatter fields).\n\n---\n\n## Failure/Default Population Rules (NFR-009)\n\nAll failure paths must produce populated contract objects. No exit path may produce an empty or null contract.\n\n1. **Step-level failure**: The step's artifact is written with failure defaults (see per-artifact table above). The step's `PortifyStepResult` records the failure with classification (timeout, missing_artifact, malformed_frontmatter, gate_failure, user_rejection, budget_exhaustion, partial_artifact).\n2. **Pipeline-level failure**: `contract.py` emits a `failed` contract with all phases populated to their last-known state.\n3. **Dry-run termination**: `contract.py` emits a `dry_run` contract with phases 3-4 marked `skipped`.\n4. **User rejection**: `contract.py` emits a `failed` contract with `user_rejection` as the failure reason.\n5. **Budget exhaustion**: `contract.py` emits a `partial` contract with `ESCALATED` convergence state and resume guidance.\n\n---\n\n## Cross-Reference to Roadmap\n\n| Artifact | Roadmap \"Artifact Outputs\" # | Step | Phase |\n|----------|------------------------------|------|-------|\n| validate-config-result.json | 1 | Step 1 | Phase 2 |\n| component-inventory.md | 2 | Step 2 | Phase 2 |\n| portify-analysis.md | 3 | Step 3 | Phase 4 |\n| portify-spec.md | 4 | Step 4 | Phase 4 |\n| Synthesized release spec | 5 | Step 5 | Phase 4 |\n| Brainstorm findings | 6 | Step 6 | Phase 5 |\n| panel-report.md | 7 | Step 7 | Phase 5 |\n| Final return contract | 8 | All | All |\n| NDJSON execution logs | 9 | All | All |\n\nAll 9 artifacts from roadmap Section \"Artifact Outputs\" are covered.\n","numLines":189,"startLine":1,"totalLines":189}}}

\"\"\"Resolve and validate the workflow path.\n\n        Returns the resolved path to the directory containing SKILL.md.\n\n        Raises:\n            FileNotFoundError: If workflow_path does not (val.startswith('\"') and val.endswith('\"')) or (","+            val.startswith(\"'\") and val.endswith(\"'\")","+        ):","+            result[key] = val[1:-1]","+        elif val.lower() in (\"true\", \"yes\"):","+            result[key] = True","+        elif val.lower() in (\"false\", \"no\"):","+            result[key] = False","+        elif val.lower() in (\"null\", \"~\", \"\"):","+            result[key] = None","+        else:","+            # Try int, then float, then string","+            try:","+                result[key] = int(val)","+            except ValueError:","+                try:","+                    result[key] = float(val)","+                except ValueError:","+                    result[key] = val","+    return result","+","+"," def
